		$(document).ready(function() {
		var showChar = 200;
		var ellipsestext = "...";
		var moretext = "More";
		var lesstext = "Less";
		$('.more').each(function() {
			var content = $(this).html();
	 
			if(content.length &gt; showChar) {
	 
				var c = content.substr(0, showChar);
				var h = content.substr(showChar-1, content.length - showChar);
	 
				var html = c + '&lt;span class="moreellipses"&gt;' + ellipsestext+ '&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="viewmorecontent"&gt;&lt;span&gt;' + h + '&lt;/span&gt;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;a href="" class="viewmorelink"&gt;' + moretext + '&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;';
	 
				$(this).html(html);
			}
	 
		});
	 
		$(".viewmorelink").click(function(){
			if($(this).hasClass("less")) {
				$(this).removeClass("less");
				$(this).html(moretext);
			} else {
				$(this).addClass("less");
				$(this).html(lesstext);
			}
			$(this).parent().prev().toggle();
			$(this).prev().toggle();
			return false;
		});
		});
  </script>

       <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function()
            {
                var my_div = $(".clickin-endofSearch");
                var search_block_top_offset = my_div.offset().top;
                var sticky_header_height = $('#clickin-headerMain').height();
                var div_top = search_block_top_offset - sticky_header_height;
                
                var topheight = $('#clickin-listingPageSearchBlockMain').height();
                
                $(window).scroll(function()
                {
                    if (div_top &lt;= $(window).scrollTop())
                    {
                        $('.clickin-headerCity').hide();
						$('.clickin-header-filter').show();
                        $('#clickin-listingPageSearchBlockMain').addClass('searchpanel-positionfxd');
                        $('#clickin-listingPageSearchBlockMain').removeClass('showsearchblock');
                        $('.clickin-endofSearchBlockMain').css('padding-top', topheight);
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        $('.clickin-headerCity').show();
						$('.clickin-header-filter').hide();
                        $('#clickin-listingPageSearchBlockMain').removeClass('searchpanel-positionfxd');
                        $('#clickin-listingPageSearchBlockMain').addClass('showsearchblock');
                        $('.clickin-endofSearchBlockMain').css('padding-top', '0px');
                    }
                });

                $(".clickin-header-filter").click(function ()
                {
                    $("#clickin-listingPageSearchBlock").slideToggle();
                    //$(".clickin-refineSearch").toggleClass("open");
                    
                    trackEvent('Refine your Search - click', 'Houses - Apartments for Sale', 'Chennai');                   
                });
            });
       </script>
